  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_6b259414-2f08-48a7-bbf7-d4b674308f6f'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2506044775" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6965527314607764662"><br/>⭐️⭐️<b>6 STARS</b>⭐️⭐️<br/><b>
  <i>”Ours is not a love story.”</i>
</b> <br/><br/>It was bound to happen, but I had no idea it would happen in such spectacular fashion. Alas, all good things come to an end....With that said, several of my #1 loves have been dethroned! My new #1, Wolfe Keaton, is <b>EVERY SINGLE LITTLE THING</b> that ever was! <br/><br/><b>The Kiss Thief</b> is unlike any other book I’ve read and is completely amazing. In fact, it’s the <b>BEST OF THE BEST! </b>I was utterly enchanted from the very first page. And just look at that gorgeous cov</span>
  <span id="freeText6965527314607764662" style="display:none"><br />⭐️⭐️<b>6 STARS</b>⭐️⭐️<br /><b>
  <i>”Ours is not a love story.”</i>
</b> <br /><br />It was bound to happen, but I had no idea it would happen in such spectacular fashion. Alas, all good things come to an end....With that said, several of my #1 loves have been dethroned! My new #1, Wolfe Keaton, is <b>EVERY SINGLE LITTLE THING</b> that ever was! <br /><br /><b>The Kiss Thief</b> is unlike any other book I’ve read and is completely amazing. In fact, it’s the <b>BEST OF THE BEST! </b>I was utterly enchanted from the very first page. And just look at that gorgeous cover. I’m <b>BLOWN AWAY</b> by the gorgeousness. L.J. Shen slays!<br /><br /><b>So...here’s what you need to know:</b><br />As I stated above, Wolfe Keaton is effing amazing! He’s, sexy, cunning, ruthless, intelligent, and driven. In short, he’s the perfect Alphahole! I’ll go on record right now and state, if alphaholes are your thing, <b>YOU WILL BE RUINED</b> by Wolfe. Prepare your hearts NOW! He’s larger than life and the ultimate BBF.<br /><br />The plot is intricately weaved like a beautiful tapestry. It’s complicated and intriguing. Unexpected twists abound. I was on the edge of my seat while reading it. And did I mention, I devoured the book at a record speed. <br /><br />The writing and storytelling are beyond reproach. Shen is one of my Top Favorite author for this very fact. I can always expect the best from her and she delivers...each and every time. <br /><br />And last but not least, the execution is fan-freaking-tastic! The feel of this book is different and so beautifully rendered. The historical inspiration shines throughout. The attention to detail and subtle nuisances that are interspersed throughout add to the decadence and beauty of the storytelling. It left me breathless and completely in awe.<br /><br />To sum up, this is my absolute favorite LJ Shen book. She raised the bar and ascended to a new level of greatness. From cover to cover, The Kiss Thief, is stunning perfection. This book has my <b>HIGHEST RECOMMENDATION.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="6965527314607764662" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2521253658" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2521253658" />
    <a title="Shabby  -BookBistroBlog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/26191846-shabby--bookbistroblog"><img alt="Shabby  -BookBistroBlog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1562639151p2/26191846.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2521253658?book_show_action=true">Dec 24, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shabby  -BookBistroBlog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shabby  -BookBistroBlog" href="/user/show/26191846-shabby--bookbistroblog">Shabby  -BookBistroBlog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2521253658" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7740374416011736590"><b>
  <i> A story of Nemesis and a villain with no chance at a happy ending.<br/>Where the Prince doesn't save the princess<br/>He tortures her.<br/>And the beauty doesn't sleep.<br/>She's stuck.<br/>In a nightmare.</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1545706486ra/26804663.gif' width='600' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Hold on to your hearts ladies cause the Big Daddy of All Predators -Wolfe Keaton has gatecrashed the Booklandia. This masked marauder is here to whisk Princess Rossi away on his Black Stallion. You will lose your hearts too, to this Brutish Buccaneer and if you're extremely lucky- your panties too in the process. </span>
  <span id="freeText7740374416011736590" style="display:none"><b>
  <i> A story of Nemesis and a villain with no chance at a happy ending.<br>Where the Prince doesn't save the princess<br>He tortures her.<br>And the beauty doesn't sleep.<br>She's stuck.<br>In a nightmare.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1545706486ra/26804663.gif" width="600" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Hold on to your hearts ladies cause the Big Daddy of All Predators -Wolfe Keaton has gatecrashed the Booklandia. This masked marauder is here to whisk Princess Rossi away on his Black Stallion. You will lose your hearts too, to this Brutish Buccaneer and if you're extremely lucky- your panties too in the process.  <br><b>
  <i>"Once a Thief ; Always a thief<br>I wanted to see for myself if the rumours of your beauty were true"</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1545705749ra/26804642.gif" width="600" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Senator Wolfe Keaton has not only stolen Princess Francesca Rossi's first kiss, he has stolen her dreams, her life and is working his way to steal her heart too. Al, these she'd been safeguarding for Angelo Bandini.<br><b>
  <i>He took the power. MY power<br>Wolfe Keaton was A KISS THIEF</i>
</b><br>If you love-hated the #HotHoles , you ain't seen nothing yet. Leigh has surpassed her earlier work in not only the gorgeous offbeat cover, but equally Fabulous off beat story too. It has a very scarlett-Rhett vibe and takes me back to my Mills &amp; Boon days. The writing is sharper, shows teeth, the vengeful notes are stabbing. Leigh doesn't shy away from flaunting his vicious intentions. He's not here to make friends. In fact he's here to make men &amp; women kneel in his presence and beg for scraps of his goodwill.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1545705749ra/26804641.gif" width="600" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Wolfe will give EVERY HOT HOLE  a run for their money. He's drop dead sexy, ruthlessly ambitious &amp; passionately patriotic. Leigh has AGAIN  proven why she's the QUEEN OF creating lickalicious ALPHAHOLES. This story is completely new in plot, setting and tone. The intricate story keeps you ON YOUR TOES throughout. It has a sinister and darker vibe. People constantly change sides and loyalties and an undercurrent of danger, betrayal and blackmail is buzzing at every step.<br><b>
  <i>"How about you give me what I really want, Rossi? Your PRIDE"</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1545705749ra/26804644.gif" width="600" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>On the other end,  Francesca is princess of the Rossi  clan-The Outfit. Born and bred to stand a step behind the men, She's polished, sophisticated and ladylike. A perfect asset to act as an arm candy to Senator on the rise in politics. She merely changes cages and a no walled prison is still suffocating as any for her crushed ambitions and dreams.<br><b>
  <i> I am an unwanted puppy, running from door to door in the pouring rain, looking for shelter </i>
</b><br>By the end of the story, the princess turns into a warrior and ends up winning your heart. Her mettle is so strong, her enemies end up underestimating the steeliness of her spine.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1545705749ra/26804643.gif" width="600" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A particular scene in the middle of the book was so cruel, it brought tears to my eyes and from that point on, both the characters seem to change their tint. The scene was quite dark and it was a catalyst in changing the course of the story. Brilliance of the scene was in the tears. You'd expect them to be of hatred, but they are of sacrifice and martyrdom.<br><b>
  <i>I am a rusty barbwire, twisted together, knotted in a ball of fear!</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1545705749ra/26804645.gif" width="600" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Francesca tops from the bottom and uplifts the scene by sheer endurance. The ensuing "Walk of Shame" is a slap on the face (you'll understand it when you read it) I swear it's akin to seeing a rough diamond being faceted and polished to sparkling brilliance right in front of your eyes. There's enough fire in her to inspire others to draw on her courage and bravery. S.U.P.E.R.B !!!<br><b>
  <i>"Leave,"<br>"I'll never doubt you again, Francesca"<br>"LEAVE!!!"</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1503746205ra/23691094.gif" width="600" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I believe LJ  was a bit apprehensive about this out-of-the-box story and I can somewhat understand. She's pushed the envelope, written scenes with sadistic pathos(you'll get it when you read it), she has shed her comfortable blanket and penned some chilling sentiments. But a lion is a lion at the end of the day, he'll starve before eating grass. so her fears will prove to be unfounded when ALL her readers-old and new will LOVE the story!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1545705749ra/26804647.gif" width="600" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This story shows a lot of growth as a writer on Leigh's part and will definitely endear her more to the readers.The noteworthy thing in Leigh's characters is that they don't change their spots. The assholes don't spout flowery monologues and fangs don't get withdrawn. The characters remain true to their traits right up til the end.<br><b>
  <i>"He's in hate with my father and in lust with me"</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1545705749ra/26804646.gif" width="600" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's an oxymoron that you love-hate these characters with equal fervour. <br>Brilliant writing, thoroughly enjoyable ride which came to an end so soon, I didn't even realise it. I wish the book went on and on and never ended. It's been ages since I read a paperback and kept the lights on, much to my husband's irritation, but I couldn't help it!! Wolfe just bit me hard and carried me away in his fangs. I hope his knees heal soon cause he has a lot of genuflecting in his future😜<br><b>
  <i>5 plates full of Humble Pie</i>
</b><br>#BookBistroBlogApproved <br>Follow us on :<br>FB - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/groups/BookBistroBlog">https://www.facebook.com/groups/BookB...</a><br>Blog -<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://bookbistroblogcom.wordpress.com">https://bookbistroblogcom.wordpress.com</a><br>Blog -<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://bookbistroblogger.blogspot.com">https://bookbistroblogger.blogspot.com</a><br>Twitter - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.twitter.com/BookBistro">https://www.twitter.com/BookBistro</a><br>Instagram - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.instagram.com/BookBistroBlog">https://www.instagram.com/BookBistroBlog</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="7740374416011736590" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2660412236" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer757201682521588825"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1550730474i/27095559._SX540_.jpg' width='420' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1546831566ra/26876321.gif' width='420' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1546930148ra/26883275.gif' width='420' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1546930148ra/26883276.gif' width='420' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1546930148ra/26883277.gif' width='420' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1546930148ra/26883278.gif' width='420' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1546930148ra/26883280.gif' width='420' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️! The Kiss Thief (stand-alone). Senator Wolfe Keaton stole a kiss, he stole her everything, or did he?!</b><br/><br/><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“All I could do was hope for his mercy. I felt safe, but not secure. Desired, but unwanted. Admired, but unloved.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br/><b>The Kiss Thief</b> (stand-alone) opens up to the mapped-out-life of nineteen-year-old mob princess <b>Francesca Rossi aka Nemesis.</b> While attending a dinner she is mocked by senator and heir <b>Wolfe Keaton aka Villain.</b> A stolen kiss later and she finds hersel</span>
  <span id="freeText757201682521588825" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1550730474i/27095559._SX540_.jpg" width="420" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1546831566ra/26876321.gif" width="420" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1546930148ra/26883275.gif" width="420" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1546930148ra/26883276.gif" width="420" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1546930148ra/26883277.gif" width="420" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1546930148ra/26883278.gif" width="420" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1546930148ra/26883280.gif" width="420" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️! The Kiss Thief (stand-alone). Senator Wolfe Keaton stole a kiss, he stole her everything, or did he?!</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“All I could do was hope for his mercy. I felt safe, but not secure. Desired, but unwanted. Admired, but unloved.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><b>The Kiss Thief</b> (stand-alone) opens up to the mapped-out-life of nineteen-year-old mob princess <b>Francesca Rossi aka Nemesis.</b> While attending a dinner she is mocked by senator and heir <b>Wolfe Keaton aka Villain.</b> A stolen kiss later and she finds herself engaged to the infuriating senator and thrown into a game of power and a quest for revenge.<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“You’re a collected debt, a retaliation, and, quite frankly, pretty decent arm candy. Good night, Miss Rossi.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>Told from dual POVs it’s an <b>enemies-to-lovers, May-December romance</b> set in the mob world. Though it may come across as a triangle, to me there was never any doubt that Wolfe could be the only hero. He’s ruthless, cunning, aloof, mysterious, blunt yet possessive. He manipulated every situation while the truth behind his contempt for the young heiress is slowly revealed.<br><br>Spectacular! Seductive! Sex-on-a-stick hero! A glued-to-your-kindle read!<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“We were entwined and entangled, connected with invisible strings, each of us trying to pull away, only to create more knots that made us closer.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>***<br>Hero: ★★★★★<br>Heroine: ★★★★★<br>Plot: ★★★★★<br>Storytelling: ★★★★★<br>Sexual tension: ★★★★★<br>Sex scenes: ★★★★★<br>Story ending: ★★★★★<br>******************************************<br><b>OVERALL RATING:</b> ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>Angst: <b>| LOW FOCUS |</b><br>Darkness: <b>| LOW FOCUS |</b><br>Humor: <b>| MEDIUM FOCUS |</b><br>Kink: <b>| MEDIUM FOCUS |</b><br>Romance: <b>| HIGH FOCUS |</b><br>Sex frequency: <b>| MEDIUM FOCUS |</b><br>Suspense: <b>| LOW FOCUS |</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1546930148ra/26883279.gif" width="420" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>ARC provided to me by author L.J. Shen in exchange for an honest review.</i>
</b></span>

<div id="review_2506030617" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2506030617" />
    <a title="Vanessa (When Vane Reads)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16230100-vanessa-when-vane-reads"><img alt="Vanessa (When Vane Reads)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594704027p2/16230100.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2506030617?book_show_action=true">Sep 20, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Vanessa (When Vane Reads)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Vanessa (When Vane Reads)" href="/user/show/16230100-vanessa-when-vane-reads">Vanessa (When Vane Reads)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16230100-vanessa-when-vane-reads?shelf=favoritos">favoritos</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16230100-vanessa-when-vane-reads?shelf=arc">arc</a>

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2506030617" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9779953746440202917"><b>English/spanish version<br/><br/>“Falling in love was so tragic. No wonder it made people so sad”</b><br/><br/>A standing ovation for <b>ONE OF THE BEST BOOKS THAT I'VE EVER READ</b>, and L.J Shen's best story to date. It left me with the worst book hangover of the year! <b>ITS INTRICATE PLOT IS A NEW BRAND OF PERFECTION SO MIND-BLOWING THAT IT WILL LEAVE YOU BREATHLESS.</b> <br/><br/>Have you ever felt that words are not enough to describe what you feel? that's me now after reading this story, I'm an emotional mess and nervous wreck. The Kis</span>
  <span id="freeText9779953746440202917" style="display:none"><b>English/spanish version<br /><br />“Falling in love was so tragic. No wonder it made people so sad”</b><br /><br />A standing ovation for <b>ONE OF THE BEST BOOKS THAT I'VE EVER READ</b>, and L.J Shen's best story to date. It left me with the worst book hangover of the year! <b>ITS INTRICATE PLOT IS A NEW BRAND OF PERFECTION SO MIND-BLOWING THAT IT WILL LEAVE YOU BREATHLESS.</b> <br /><br />Have you ever felt that words are not enough to describe what you feel? that's me now after reading this story, I'm an emotional mess and nervous wreck. The Kiss Thief, * sigh *, is EPIC BEYOND WORDS. Oh God, I loved every second when I read it. It's so different from everything I've read before, but so completely addictive. The first words had me hooked on the story and turning the pages as if my life depended on it. <b>I COULD NOT PUT IT DOWN!!!! </b><br /><br />The plot and the characters consumed me, obsessed me, hypnotized me, with an emotional and harrowing romance bordering the dark and raw, full of love, banter, hatred, passion, opulence, power, anguish, that kept me on the edge of the seat, heart racing and a swarm of butterflies inside me stomach. <br /><br />Get ready for the most ruthless alpha male ever, more than Troy and Vicious together. Wolfe Keaton is despicable, cruel, he has no mercy for anyone, he also is sooooo sexy, he melted my panties, gave me goosebumps and made me blush several times. But nevertheless, he captured my heart. He loves so hard, the sweet way he protects and cares for the heroine, wow, I'm dying of love for him, he's my new obsession. <b>MY TOP BOOK BOYFRIEND EVER!!! </b><br /><br />Francesca is a sweet, beautiful, brave and strong girl who melted my heart, her way of talking to the plants made me laugh out loud, she also faces situations with courage. She is everything I look for in a heroine. I LOVE HER!! <br /><br />The explosive attraction and passion between the characters is unparalleled, and the slow burn, let me tell you, it reaches stratospheric levels, it could burn a whole room. I cannot get enough of them, I still cannot get them out of my head. <b> THEIR ROMANCE IS SOOO TEAR-JERKING, SO PASSIONATE AND EMOTIONAL, </b> everything what I am looking for in a romance, ahhhh, I keep sighing. <br /><br /><b>WITH AN EXQUISITE AND FLAWLESS PROSE, L.J. SHEN MANAGES TO CREATE A MASTERPIECE THAT REACHES YOUR SOUL. </b> A masterfully written story that evokes so many different feelings in the reader. Mrs. Shen continues to prove why she is the best storyteller. She has an ability to wrap you with her words and catch your heart, smash it, tear it completely and break it into pieces. My soul still does not recover from the suffering. THIS LOVE STORY IS SO EPIC, SO HEARTBREAKINGLY BEAUTIFUL THAT I NOT WANT TO LEAVE THIS WORLD OR THE CHARACTERS. <br /><br />It is definitely a must read. An exquisite romance that you will not want to miss. What are you waiting for? Go read it now!<br /><br /><br /><b>Versión en español</b><br />Una ovación de pie para UNO DE LOS MEJORES LIBROS QUE HE LEÍDO y la mejor historia de L.J. Shen hasta la fecha. ¡Me dejó con la peor resaca literaria del año! SU INTRINCADA TRAMA ES UNA NUEVA MARCA DE PERFECCIÓN TAN EXTRAORDINARIA QUE TE DEJARÁ SIN RESPIRACIÓN.<br /><br />¿Alguna vez has sentido que las palabras no son suficientes para describir lo que sientes? esa soy yo ahora después de leer esta historia, soy un lío emocional y nervioso. The Kiss Thief, *suspiro*, es EPICA más allá de las palabras. Oh Dios, amé cada segundo al leerlo. Es tan diferente de todo lo que he leído antes pero tan completamente adictivo. Las primeras palabras me tuvieron enganchada a la historia y volteando las páginas como si mi vida dependiera de ello. ¡NO PUDE PONERLO ABAJO!<br /><br />La trama y los personajes me consumieron, me obsesionaron, me hipnotizaron, un romance emocional bordeando lo oscuro y crudo, lleno de amor, odio, pasión, opulencia, poder, angustia, que me mantuvo al borde del asiento, el corazón acelerado y un enjambre de mariposas dentro de mi estómago. <br /><br />Y prepárense para el macho alfa más despiadado de la historia, más que Troy y Vicious juntos. Wow, Wolfe Keaton es despreciable, cruel, no tiene piedad de nadie, sin embargo, es increíblemente sexy, derritió mis pantaletas, me provocó piel de gallina y me hizo sonrojar varias veces. Pero a pesar de todo, él capturó mi corazón. Él ama con tanta fuerza, la forma en que la protege y cuida a la heroína, muero de amor por él, es mi nueva obsesión. EL MEJOR NOVIO LITERARIO DE TODOS LOS TIEMPOS.<br /><br />Francesca es una chica dulce, bella, valiente y fuerte que me derritió el corazón, su forma de hablarle a las plantas me hizo reír a carcajadas, pero además ella enfrenta las situaciones con coraje. Ella es todo lo que busco en una heroína ¡¡LA AMO!!<br /><br />La atracción explosiva y pasión entre los personajes no tiene comparación, hierve a fuego lento, y déjenme decirles, alcanza niveles estratosféricos, ufff esos podrían incendiar una habitación completa. No puedo conseguir suficiente de ellos, todavía no me los puedo sacar de la cabeza. SU ROMANCE ES TAN DESGARRADOR, TAN APASIONADO Y EMOCIONAL, AHHHH, todo lo que busco en un romance. Sigo suspirando.<br /><br />CON UNA PROSA EXQUISITA E HIPNÓTICA, L.J. SHEN LOGRA CREAR UNA OBRA MAESTRA QUE LLEGA A TU ALMA. Una historia magistralmente escrita que evoca tantos diferentes sentimientos en el lector. Ella sigue probando porque es la mejor en lo que hace. Tiene la habilidad de envolverte con sus palabras y atrapar tu corazón, hacerlo un puño y desgarrarlo completamente, pisotearlo, y hacerlo pedazos. Mi alma todavía no se recupera de tanto sufrimiento. ESTA HISTORIA DE AMOR ES TAN ÉPICA, TAN DESGARRADORAMENTE HERMOSA QUE NO QUIERO DEJAR SU MUNDO O LOS PERSONAJES. <br /><br />Definitivamente es una lectura obligatoria. Una historia épica y exquisita que no te querrás perder. ¿Qué estás esperando? Ve a leerlo ahora.</span>

</blockquote><br>If you like a modern day arranged marriage trope, welcome to your next addiction. This book? GAH! It had an anti-hero that only Shen can write; brutal and hard but completely redeemable. This is someone you won't be able to help rooting for! This was like if <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/30839185.Vicious__Sinners_of_Saint___1_" title="Vicious (Sinners of Saint, #1) by L.J. Shen" rel="nofollow noopener">Vicious</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/27263454.Sparrow" title="Sparrow by L.J. Shen" rel="nofollow noopener">Sparrow</a> had a baby, and that baby threw down the gauntlet of delicious angst and grit. A clashing of a ruthless politician and the mafia, and a young beauty used as a pawn that gets caught in the crosshairs of political agendas and blackmail. <br><br>Francesca Rossi was such a breath of fresh air. For someone so young, she had this endearing naiveté to her that was beneath her hardened persona. She's not a doormat, even when dealing with an extremely dominant man. This is not a woman that takes things lying down. She's sharp-witted and smart-mouthed. I absolutely loved her.<br><br>The Kiss Thief was a book that kept me riveted to the pages from beginning to end. It was unlike any book I've read in a long damn while and it was absolutely everything. EVERYTHING, I tells ya! <br><br>I know you're thinking, Lana, you're being vague as hell right now. But trust me, you don't need or WANT to know more. This is a book that you NEED to go into absolutely blind, or you'll do yourself a great disservice. <div id="review_2506042226" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2506042226" />
    <a title="Lisa (Two Bookish Brits)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/35250232-lisa-two-bookish-brits"><img alt="Lisa (Two Bookish Brits)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514810940p2/35250232.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2506042226?book_show_action=true">Dec 28, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lisa (Two Bookish Brits)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lisa (Two Bookish Brits)" href="/user/show/35250232-lisa-two-bookish-brits">Lisa (Two Bookish Brits)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35250232-lisa-two-bookish-brits?shelf=enemies-to-lovers">enemies-to-lovers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2506042226" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18314009855201424594">Oh wow, wow, wow. I’m in awe right now. <br/><br/>If you’re a lover of L.J. Shen’s Hotholes then The Kiss Thief is going to be exactly what you want because ladies (and gents), we have a new alphahole in town. Mr Wolfe Keaton, the man that makes men quiver in their boots and women drop to their knees. He’s sexy as sin with an attitude to go with it. He’s ruthless and harsh and keeps his true feelings locked away. <br/><br/>The Kiss Thief isn’t your typical romance. It’s a story about a nemesis and a villain. One th</span>
  <span id="freeText18314009855201424594" style="display:none">Oh wow, wow, wow. I’m in awe right now. <br /><br />If you’re a lover of L.J. Shen’s Hotholes then The Kiss Thief is going to be exactly what you want because ladies (and gents), we have a new alphahole in town. Mr Wolfe Keaton, the man that makes men quiver in their boots and women drop to their knees. He’s sexy as sin with an attitude to go with it. He’s ruthless and harsh and keeps his true feelings locked away. <br /><br />The Kiss Thief isn’t your typical romance. It’s a story about a nemesis and a villain. One that starts with hate and anger, with pain and heartache and turns in to so much more than you could ever expect. A romance that has you gritting your teeth and ready to pull your hair out in frustration. One that has you melting on the spot and clutching at your heart because of all the emotions it inflicts upon you. <br /><br />This story is incredible, one that I won’t be giving away. You <b>HAVE</b> to experience this book through fresh eyes and no spoilers to 100% enjoy it and enjoy it you will. <br /><br />LJ Shen has gone and written a book that’s far from her normal style of writing and absolutely slayed it like the queen she is. Leigh, hands down, takes the crown for writing <b>THE BEST ALPHAHOLES</b> in book land. <br /><br />Since the announcement of this book and the updates from Leigh I’ve been eager to read it but I wasn’t ready for what she gave us, it was definitely a pleasant surprise. The amount of time, effort and love that’s gone in to this book shines brightly and I’m in awe of this woman, she’s truly incredible. <br /><br />This book is most definitely my favourite book from this author. My favourite read of 2018 and no doubt my favourite book from 2019. TKT is everything I love about romance’s. The struggles and the real ness of it all hooked me from the get go. If I could give this beauty a higher rating than 5, I would. It deserves all the stars and more.</span>

<div id="review_2506032750" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2506032750" />
    <a title="Sarah - Musings of the Modern Belle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8648577-sarah---musings-of-the-modern-belle"><img alt="Sarah - Musings of the Modern Belle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1516857517p2/8648577.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2506032750?book_show_action=true">Sep 23, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sarah - Musings of the Modern Belle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sarah - Musings of the Modern Belle" href="/user/show/8648577-sarah---musings-of-the-modern-belle">Sarah - Musings of the Modern Belle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2506032750" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3414446062713240612">***AVAILABLE NOW - FULL REVIEW***<br/><br/>MY FIRST FAVORITE AND MUST READ OF 2019<br/><br/>5+ Nemesis CROWNS<br/><br/>LJ Shen has rocked me world, tilted it on its axis, and I don’t which way is up or down after the whirlwind she just took me on. The Kiss Thief is EVERYTHING I love in a romance, and I never wanted this book to end. EVER! <br/><br/>Wolfe Keaton has taken top book boyfriend spot. With his confidence and intelligence and lethal charisma, I was utterly charmed by this man. His cold exterior makes him seem untouchable and</span>
  <span id="freeText3414446062713240612" style="display:none">***AVAILABLE NOW - FULL REVIEW***<br /><br />MY FIRST FAVORITE AND MUST READ OF 2019<br /><br />5+ Nemesis CROWNS<br /><br />LJ Shen has rocked me world, tilted it on its axis, and I don’t which way is up or down after the whirlwind she just took me on. The Kiss Thief is EVERYTHING I love in a romance, and I never wanted this book to end. EVER! <br /><br />Wolfe Keaton has taken top book boyfriend spot. With his confidence and intelligence and lethal charisma, I was utterly charmed by this man. His cold exterior makes him seem untouchable and callous, but the way he takes care of the heroine, even if it seems detached, shows he is a man who has the capability to love, and love he does. The evolution of his character, the freedom of forgiving and letting go, is so inspirational. This is man who has been wronged and instead of continuing to revel in the ashes, he rises from the love and affection to create something better and beautiful. He is willing to fall to his knees and relinquish what has held him together for love. What is more romantic than that? He has my heart. TOP BOOK BOYFRIEND material right here. <br /><br />Francesca is a heroine, like most of Leigh’s, that has an inner strength. Like most of the secondary characters in the story, readers might see her as weak and docile but not all who are silent are weak, and Francesca is the farthest thing from complacent. She takes power when she can and yields it like a weapon. She pushes those who try to control her and speaks with actions when she knows her voice will be ignored. This woman who may not show her strength on the outside is stronger than any character LJ Shen has written to date. I couldn’t be more enamored with this tiny but mighty sprite of a character. <br /><br />The Kiss Thief is more than my words can articulate. There is the romantic layer with hot sex and swooning declarations of love (eventually). There is the danger and the vengeance that will keep readers turning the pages. But with this book, Shen layers it with an allusion to mythology while also contemplating ideas of revenge and forgiveness and how one lifts you up and the other tears you down. If those layers aren’t enough, Shen continues to astound with her reflection on what real love is, which is letting someone you love be free, having them stay by choice versus keeping them prisoner. Real love allows for freedom and growth, evolution and change. It is an absolutely masterpiece that had me riveted from the moment these two meet and an HEA that will steal your soul and leave a smile on your face. <br /><br />Leigh Shen continues to prove why she is a best seller. She integrates romance with real ideas that deal with the heart and the mind. She creates characters that consume us and loves that are so epic it shifts our world. I never ever want to leave this world or these people! I have a new Shen favorite! <br /><br />Beta read</span>
  <a data-text-id="3414446062713240612" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/82040775-emma?shelf=didn-t-finish">didn-t-finish</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2617847823" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13017671967018330182">Surprise! Surprise! There's no surprises in this book. We have the same characters and plot, again. To be fair the book was engaging and well written. The MCs had great chemistry. Those things might be enough for you to enjoy and I didn't finish the book, so I might not be a fair judge.<br/><br/>The amount of sexism, double standards and cliché was disturbing and unbearable for me. His thoughts about sex and women were vomit inducing. And her insecurity because she is inexperienced virgin were cringe wort</span>
  <span id="freeText13017671967018330182" style="display:none">Surprise! Surprise! There's no surprises in this book. We have the same characters and plot, again. To be fair the book was engaging and well written. The MCs had great chemistry. Those things might be enough for you to enjoy and I didn't finish the book, so I might not be a fair judge.<br /><br />The amount of sexism, double standards and cliché was disturbing and unbearable for me. His thoughts about sex and women were vomit inducing. And her insecurity because she is inexperienced virgin were cringe worthy. And don't let me start about the gendered norms and expectations. I just can't!<br /><br />What I hated about the book is what I hated about every book I have read by the author. Instead of coming up with something new she is recycling her work again and again. And it's not that pleasant to begin with. And the blurb is misleading, it's not really a love triangle. The other man is just there to cause jealousy and stupid drama.<br /><br />The male lead is a manwhore jerk and the female is that pure kind girl with a fake backbone. They hate each other; op drama; they have angry sex; they fall in love; they hurt each other; more op drama; love confessions and then hea... Wait, I didn't get that far. I think I stopped around the 'hating each other' part which took way too long. Still, I don't think I'm wrong. Please correct me if I'm. <br /><br />I don't remember once when the male lead was a decent human being in this author's books, when his thoughts didn't repulse me and his actions didn't irritate me. He always arrogant, mean and hurtful. Not once he kept it in his pants after meeting the heroine and the worst, the female lead is always aware that he is having sex at the moment if she is not watching. <br /><br />I can't recall once when the heroine didn't turn boneless the moment the male mc touched her, doesn't matter what she thought or felt about him. She always plays strong and cool but fails miserably when strength and common sense are needed. And she never wins in the dominance game between her and him, never.</span>

</a><b> MY REVIEW: </b> can also be found on my blog: <br/> <a href='https://katfenton.blogspot.com/2019/01/arc-review-kiss-thief-by-lj-shen.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <b> ➽ KITTY KATS CRAZY ABOUT BOOKS</b>
</a><br/><br/><b>' 5 THE BIG BAD WOLFE STARS '</b><br/><br/><i>
  <b> A story of a Nemesis and a Villain with no chance at a happy ending. Where the prince doesn't save the princess. He tortures her. And the beauty doesn't sleep. She's stuck. In a nightmare. </b>
</i><br/><br/><b> THE KISS THIEF: </b> Is a full length contemporary Romance novel. Spoken in Dual Perspectives. <br/><br/>It all started with a wooden chest carved and made by a witch encasing three notes which would</span>
  <span id="freeText16140504199090600857" style="display:none"><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2v9sp77" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1546645425i/26859959._SX540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2zehutf" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1546645751i/26859965._SX540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=105tdtg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1545001274i/26757170.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b> MY REVIEW: </b> can also be found on my blog: <br> <a href="https://katfenton.blogspot.com/2019/01/arc-review-kiss-thief-by-lj-shen.html" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <b> ➽ KITTY KATS CRAZY ABOUT BOOKS</b>
</a><br><br><b>' 5 THE BIG BAD WOLFE STARS '</b><br><br><i>
  <b> A story of a Nemesis and a Villain with no chance at a happy ending. Where the prince doesn't save the princess. He tortures her. And the beauty doesn't sleep. She's stuck. In a nightmare. </b>
</i><br><br><b> THE KISS THIEF: </b> Is a full length contemporary Romance novel. Spoken in Dual Perspectives. <br><br>It all started with a wooden chest carved and made by a witch encasing three notes which would predict her future..The first note said <i>'I was going to be kissed by the love of my life.'</i><br><br>This was utterly unique, utterly un-put-down-able, utterly captivating, and utterly memorable, utter perfection. I couldn’t put it down, I didn’t want to put it down, I devoured this, I inhaled this, I loved this more than words can convey, L.J. Shen has got her grooooove back and she is un-stop-able!! What a way to set the new year on fire!! A little old fashioned story that will capture your heart, set your panties afire, and leave you gasping for more.<br><br>The heroine is like nothing I have ever encountered before, she’s polished, sophisticated, a socialite by name, born in a gilded cage, risking escape would result in death. A chimney smoking character that will win your heart in many ways.<br><br>This starts off with nineteen year old Francesca getting initiated into the Chicagoan Society by allowing her to pick her own husband from thousands of eligible men affiliated from the Outfit. Instead of college she was choosing the perfect husband. But she already knew within her heart who was going to be of her choosing, <br><br>And that man was Angelo, she’s known him since birth.<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2wbuc87" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1546496793ra/26851651.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The Masquerade theme was gods and goddesses, Francesca had chosen to go as Nemesis the goddess of retribution.<br><br><i>
  <b>They say your first kiss should be earned. Mine was stolen by a devil in a masquerade mask under the black Chicago sky.</b>
</i><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2qt8ep1" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1546496793ra/26851652.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>A kiss that was mean't for her chosen was stolen from her, and the man responsible was thirty year old Senator Wolfe Keaton, the most desirable man in Chicago, this one kiss set the ball rolling into unknown charters. <br><br><i>
  <b> It was just a stupid, fun tradition. Hardly a scientific fact. Surely, not all the predictions written on the notes turned out to be true. I probably wouldn't even see Wolfe Keaton ever again. </b>
</i><br><br>This set the pace perfectly, retaliation, retribution, a debt paid in full..<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2uqoug4" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1546648747i/26860121._SY540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This book right here was one of my most highly anticipated books, I couldn't wait for 2018 to be over with, I wasn't so patient to get my hands on it, I stalked the ass off it, the teasers made that anticipation the times worse, and then finally I got it in my grabby little hands and all my expectations were exceeded, I inhaled it, I devoured it, I went into this with eyes wide open and at the end of it my heart was filled to the brim. All the feels in the world, 'The Kiss Thief' was full of insane chemistry, love and angst. I adored this book! It reminded me exactly why I’m obsessed with this authors words. L.J. Shen writes the most compelling stories, and this one is my all time favourite from her.<br><br>* Teaser used is off the Authors Facebook Page * <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2e0pm6g" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1517634761i/24993460._SX540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=s3ftsk" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1545185430i/26769555.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2a0guva" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1515981059i/24879210._SX540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br> <blockquote> <div>
<a href="http://katfenton.blogspot.co.nz/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1511218918i/24493308.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <a href="mailto:kiwinz001@hotmail.com" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1511218918i/24493307.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a>  <a href="https://www.facebook.com/kittykats003/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1511218918i/24493310.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <a href="https://plus.google.com/107310326196782383941" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1511218918i/24493311.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <a href="https://twitter.com/KitKatCrzyBooks" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1511218918i/24493309.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a>

<div id="review_2640176592" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2640176592" />
    <a title="Bookgasms Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/60005052-bookgasms-book-blog"><img alt="Bookgasms Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1520259605p2/60005052.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2640176592?book_show_action=true">Dec 26, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bookgasms Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bookgasms Book Blog" href="/user/show/60005052-bookgasms-book-blog">Bookgasms Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/60005052-bookgasms-book-blog?shelf=ratula">ratula</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2640176592" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6173916869244880731">Gah!! You guys!! The Kiss Thief was everything we've come to expect from L.J. Shen and more!! BEYOND PHENOMENAL!! It was emotional, poignant and gut wrenching and filled with a brilliant story that had me glued to every page. It was so perfectly written with every intricate detail written with the utmost care. This is without a doubt THE BEST novel this author has written!!<br/><br/>Without giving away any spoilers, Shen did it once again with Wolfe Keaton. He undoubtedly is the new alpha-hole to top and </span>
  <span id="freeText6173916869244880731" style="display:none">Gah!! You guys!! The Kiss Thief was everything we've come to expect from L.J. Shen and more!! BEYOND PHENOMENAL!! It was emotional, poignant and gut wrenching and filled with a brilliant story that had me glued to every page. It was so perfectly written with every intricate detail written with the utmost care. This is without a doubt THE BEST novel this author has written!!<br /><br />Without giving away any spoilers, Shen did it once again with Wolfe Keaton. He undoubtedly is the new alpha-hole to top and that is a very tough title to win. He is dark and foreboding with an icy and unfeeling exterior. But his demeanor hides the heat and fire inside him. I absolutely FLOVED him as he was the perfect combination of hardened and vulnerable. He was consumed with vengeance and yet allowed an encounter with his enemy's daughter to set him on an impulsive journey filled with love, lust, revenge and obsession.<br /><br />Francesca Rossi likewise was absolutely astounding. She was Wolfe's perfect match and my favorite Shen heroine to date. She was strong and resilient. Delicate and beautiful in appearance but with a deep and unwavering core strength - choosing to write her own story with the cards she is dealt in life by unequivocally making it her own. She was completely underestimated by all the men in her life and the lasting impression she would make on all of them.<br /><br />Overall The Kiss Thief was truly phenomenal and another feather in the cap of this remarkable author. Her brilliance is apparent in every novel she puts out where each book is better than her last and her skills are only surpassed by her goals to better her craft, which she accomplishes every time. She needs to officially rename herself Slay Shen because she always kills it. Bravo! 6 stars! ~Ratula</span>
  <a data-text-id="6173916869244880731" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_2617989836" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2617989836" />
    <a title="Melanie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3030788-melanie"><img alt="Melanie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577914102p2/3030788.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2617989836?book_show_action=true">Dec 06, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melanie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melanie" href="/user/show/3030788-melanie">Melanie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=read-in-2019">read-in-2019</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=erotic-scenes">erotic-scenes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=buddy-reads">buddy-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2617989836" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15423055250109255207"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1550120832i/27060534._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“A story of a Nemesis and a Villain with no chance at a happy ending.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>Francesca Rossi thought she had her life already figured out, even though she was only nineteen, and regardless of what kind of life she has ever wanted for herself. Her father is very powerful and has built an empire in Chicago, even if he deals with and in some very dark things. And Francesca’s hand in marriage is going to be connection to another powerful family one day. And it appears that the day is coming ver</span>
  <span id="freeText15423055250109255207" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1550120832i/27060534._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“A story of a Nemesis and a Villain with no chance at a happy ending.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Francesca Rossi thought she had her life already figured out, even though she was only nineteen, and regardless of what kind of life she has ever wanted for herself. Her father is very powerful and has built an empire in Chicago, even if he deals with and in some very dark things. And Francesca’s hand in marriage is going to be connection to another powerful family one day. And it appears that the day is coming very quickly. <br><br>Angelo Bandini is the boy that Francesca has grown up with, and now he is the man that she believes she will share her life with. He is safe, he is dependable, and he has been a constant in her life for as long as she can remember, even if he has never given her a real kiss before. <br><br>Wolfe Keaton is a very powerful senator, and he and his lifelong vendetta are about to ruin everything at a masquerade party that they are all attending. Especially since Francesca stole one of the notes that are passed down from the women in her family, but they are supposed to be kept locked away in a chest for their wedding day. And those notes are supposed to completely predict and/or alter your fate. <br><br>And the note that Francesca pulled the night of the masquerade said that she was going to be kissed by the love of her life. Which she completely assumes will mean that Angelo is finally going to give her the kiss she has dreamed of her entire life. But Wolfe and his grudge have very different plans in mind. And all the angst ensues, along with a promise of marriage. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“But, my darling, that’s the difference between me and your father. I never pretended to deserve you. I simply took you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I actually really enjoyed this story so much. I loved the angst, I loved the romance, and I really ended up loving the characters. But the first sex scene in this is honestly one of the most sus things I’ve ever read in my life. Francesca was truly being so stupid, and the lie she told to make a point? It truly took a year off my life. Also, Wolfe not understanding the basic concept of birth control, while pretending he did, took an extra year off my life. <br><br>But besides these two things? I honestly loved this and completely recommend. Especially if you like a good alpha dude, because Wolfe is literally the epitome of that. I had a blast while reading this, and was so pleasantly surprised to finish and realize that it was a standalone, too. If you’re looking for some sexy dirty talk, a whole lot of angst, and a little romance, then I completely recommend this one. <br><br><a href="https://meltotheany.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/meltotheany/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://www.twitter.com/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://meltotheany.tumblr.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a> | <a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UC4RbHEg_fH6CewJrh_0xJ9g" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a> | <a href="http://www.twitch.tv/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitch</a> <br><br><b>Content and trigger warnings</b> for use of the term sp*rit animal, some weird discourse about food and dieting, talk of loss of a loved one, domestic abuse and talk of cheating (not involving the main characters), murder, attempted murder, grey area cheating, and a very unpleasant virgin sex scene. <br><br>Buddy Read with <a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UCQBtjMbFlM1oI0ImK8BH7wQ" rel="nofollow noopener">Myonna</a> &amp; <a href="https://www.youtube.com/user/rilaaaay1" rel="nofollow noopener">Riley</a>! ❤ <br><br>❤ I also read this for <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=R8dAwl_IMMY&amp;t=" rel="nofollow noopener">Contemporary-a-thon</a>!</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2513102090?book_show_action=true">Jan 04, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica ❥Chatterbooks Book Blog❥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica ❥Chatterbooks Book Blog❥" href="/user/show/37057510-jessica-chatterbooks-book-blog">Jessica ❥Chatterbooks Book Blog❥</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/43492490-the-kiss-thief">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/37057510-jessica-chatterbooks-book-blog?shelf=mafia">mafia</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/37057510-jessica-chatterbooks-book-blog?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/37057510-jessica-chatterbooks-book-blog?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/37057510-jessica-chatterbooks-book-blog?shelf=arranged-marriage">arranged-marriage</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2513102090" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4609477193593060797">It's no secret that The Kiss Thief was one of my most anticipated releases of 2019. L. J. Shen is one of my favorite authors of all time, and I look forward to every single book she publishes. This time was a little different though. The mystery surrounding this book and the collective excitement of all of the other L. J. fans I knew took it to a whole new level!<br/><br/><a href='https://beta.photobucket.com/u/majikmommie/p/b6adda49-92b4-4379-bbd6-778892c7d0e6' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1547811316ra/26935724.gif' alt='tumblr_omgt4bhxy01tf6696o2_500' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> </a><br/><br/>All the time wondering what the story would be about, what the name of it was, and basically, everything else about this book had alr</span>
  <span id="freeText4609477193593060797" style="display:none">It's no secret that The Kiss Thief was one of my most anticipated releases of 2019. L. J. Shen is one of my favorite authors of all time, and I look forward to every single book she publishes. This time was a little different though. The mystery surrounding this book and the collective excitement of all of the other L. J. fans I knew took it to a whole new level!<br><br><a href="https://beta.photobucket.com/u/majikmommie/p/b6adda49-92b4-4379-bbd6-778892c7d0e6" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1547811316ra/26935724.gif" alt="tumblr_omgt4bhxy01tf6696o2_500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </a><br><br>All the time wondering what the story would be about, what the name of it was, and basically, everything else about this book had already made for so much anticipation I could barely stand it. Then once I found out the answers to all of those things, it just made it worse!<br><br><a href="https://beta.photobucket.com/u/majikmommie/p/eb3840e7-7242-485a-9357-1855cb277222" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1547811252ra/26935723.gif" alt="c9695099bda0169c3f1094ff9afca4af" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </a><br><br>An enemies to lovers story with an arranged marriage, a love triangle, and the mafia?! It was like she wrote this book just for me! I was ready to pay Leigh any sum of money she wanted for an early copy of this book. I thought I was going to legit lose my shit if I didn't get my hands on it soon! Patience is just not a virtue I possess. <br><br><a href="https://beta.photobucket.com/u/majikmommie/p/2f81dd04-f175-496b-bd79-4c05c5d50bb0" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1547811352ra/26935726.gif" alt="anigif_enhanced-buzz-27003-1410791751-4" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </a><br><br>All that build up could have set the stage for a let down of epic proportions. I wouldn't have been surprised if it did. Having expectations like that can ruin almost anything, but guess what? It didn't. Not only did The Kiss Thief not disappoint me in the least, it completely blew me away! Every expectation I had was met and exceeded! I was on cloud fucking nine the entire time I read it.<br><br><a href="https://beta.photobucket.com/u/majikmommie/p/ae2c21b9-bd87-4301-b0ae-d6f489be48ec" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1547811440ra/26935729.gif" alt="Eo5J" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </a><br><br>This author's writing is mesmerizing and just downright magical. I'm so in awe of her talent it's ridiculous. I basically highlight everything and drool as I read at this point. There are no words that can adequately describe how incredible it is.<br><blockquote>
  <a href="https://beta.photobucket.com/u/majikmommie/p/bc5064cd-34d3-4231-b194-a08b39a975b1" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1547811398ra/26935727.gif" alt="tt-1" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </a>
</blockquote><br>I absolutely adored everything about this novel. I couldn't be more enamored with it if I tried. The setting, the characters, the plot, and the steam are all nothing less than utter perfection. I was engaged throughout the entirety of the book, and it gave me all the feels. My emotions ran the gamut from laughter to anger to tears. I could feel my heart break, mend, and warm over and over again, and I never wanted it to end.<br><br><a href="https://beta.photobucket.com/u/majikmommie/p/7a7e4169-afc2-48e1-9fc6-acb2af2b1b50" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1547811508ra/26935734.gif" alt="872953" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </a><br><br>Before I get even more carried away and blabber on further about my love affair with L. J. Shen, I want to talk about my favorite part of this book, the characters. Francesca and Wolfe are an unlikely pair, but at the same time, perfectly matched. They're complex individuals that bring out the best in each other, challenge each other, and understand one another like no one else. From their very first meeting, the chemistry between them was insane, and it just escalated from there.<br><br><a href="https://beta.photobucket.com/u/majikmommie/p/f5b83e23-28a7-47ee-a6dc-d4e9989ed5c7" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1547811579ra/26935735.gif" alt="tumblr_njf2zvLDDJ1r2p77io1_500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </a><br><br>Francesca is a different type of heroine than I've read from this author before, and I enjoyed that. I loved her transformation from the slightly immature, sheltered, unsure, naive teenager in the beginning to the strong, resilient, confident young woman she was by the end. That being said, she was more than meets the eye even from the start, but nobody saw it. It didn't take long for Wolfe to though, and boy, did he like what he saw! <br><br><a href="https://beta.photobucket.com/u/majikmommie/p/8d736dea-9cab-4d32-b230-afbc2bb6a09c" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1547811765ra/26935742.gif" alt="Bki" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </a><br><br>Wolfe is one of my favorite asshole heroes Leigh has ever created, and that's saying a lot since she writes some of the best I've ever read. He's sexy, intelligent, cocky, complicated, and all alpha. His main priority is always to protect and care for Francesca above all else, and when it comes to sex, the man knows what he's doing. Powerful, loyal, slightly broken, morally gray, and swoonworthy af, Wolfe is everything I could want in a hero. If you love Vicious and Troy, you will fall head over heels Wolfe. No doubt about it!<br><br><a href="https://beta.photobucket.com/u/majikmommie/p/991f00d4-ecb6-4980-967b-5f9dec4ff3c0" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1547811579ra/26935736.gif" alt="jji" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </a><br><br>Captivating, addictive, and fantastically written, The Kiss Thief should be on the must read list of every fan of contemporary romance. It is one of the best books L. J. Shen has ever written. I can say without a shadow of a doubt, this is going to be on my favorites of 2019 list and plenty of other author people's, too.<br><br><a href="https://beta.photobucket.com/u/majikmommie/p/8c8c5c6e-f74d-41b8-bfe9-0979f873c76c" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1547811579ra/26935737.gif" alt="black-swan-perfect" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </a><br><br>Side note: I know some readers tend to shy away from love triangles, but if you're one of them, I wouldn't let that hold you back from picking this one up. You don't have anything to worry about in my opinion.<br><br><a href="https://beta.photobucket.com/u/majikmommie/p/c456a294-1260-4553-a4f3-05c889f60273" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1547811579ra/26935738.gif" alt="hii-2" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </a><br><br>If you're a fan of this author's work, asshole heroes, and/or enemies to lovers romance, this one's for you!    </span>
  <a data-text-id="4609477193593060797" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3113734393?book_show_action=true">Jan 03, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="jessica" class="user" itemprop="url" name="jessica" href="/user/show/10171516-jessica">jessica</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781732624719" href="/book/show/43540348-the-kiss-thief">review of another edition</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3113734393" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8950615761285389469">if you asked me why i picked this up, i couldnt even make up a excuse. it was an impulsive and mindless decision, just like my choice to continue reading it. <br/><br/>i found a lot of things wrong about this book, but the biggest thing that was so off-putting to me was the unbelievable ‘romance.’ not the unrealistic plot, not the immature characters, not the lackluster writing. its the fact that the reader is told the two MCs are in love with other but there is NO PROOF to support this idea. maybe im jus</span>
  <span id="freeText8950615761285389469" style="display:none">if you asked me why i picked this up, i couldnt even make up a excuse. it was an impulsive and mindless decision, just like my choice to continue reading it. <br /><br />i found a lot of things wrong about this book, but the biggest thing that was so off-putting to me was the unbelievable ‘romance.’ not the unrealistic plot, not the immature characters, not the lackluster writing. its the fact that the reader is told the two MCs are in love with other but there is NO PROOF to support this idea. maybe im just not a fan of the whole ‘guy asks like a massive a-hole but its okay because he has a tortured past and if you do what he says, he may not verbally abuse you’ trope. i guess kindness is a component i need when it comes to my romance stories. <br /><br />but with that being said, i could not put this down. and i actually enjoyed reading this, even if the story is flawed. no idea how or why, but this did entertain me to an extent. <br /><br /><b>↠ <i>2.5 stars</i></b></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2651748973" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer11847524113078199949"><b>Listen, I've had it. I can't sympathize anymore. We've given authors enough and more chances to redeem themselves and stop hating their female characters. It's 2019 & this is BS. I can't read such pathetic heroines anymore. All the writers need to grow up because the readers certainly have a long time back. You have to be one step ahead of your readers not 5 steps behind. <br/>5 chapters in and I just couldn't seem to go on. Forced myself to to reach 15. But no more.<br/>And please God that age gap & how </b></span>
  <span id="freeText11847524113078199949" style="display:none"><b>Listen, I've had it. I can't sympathize anymore. We've given authors enough and more chances to redeem themselves and stop hating their female characters. It's 2019 &amp; this is BS. I can't read such pathetic heroines anymore. All the writers need to grow up because the readers certainly have a long time back. You have to be one step ahead of your readers not 5 steps behind. <br />5 chapters in and I just couldn't seem to go on. Forced myself to to reach 15. But no more.<br />And please God that age gap &amp; how he treated her. The girl is 19 &amp; the guy is 31. Fine . No problem. But the way he spoke to her is BS man. You can't promote such things with that age gap. I know there is a certain reader base for exactly this category of asshole but at least make sure you give the girl an age &gt;19 so that teens who read this shit don't get influenced to fall in love with morons in real life. <br />Because all of us with half a functioning brain know that if our sisters/daughters/mothers were talked to this way, there'd be handprints of a tight slap on each cheek of the guy. <br />I AM SO DONE WITH PATHETIC CHARACTERS. Been raging about this on Goodreads for almost 4 years now.</b></span>

<div id="review_2720469228" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2720469228" />
    <a title="ELLIAS (elliasreads)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13699205-ellias-elliasreads"><img alt="ELLIAS (elliasreads)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1580549084p2/13699205.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2720469228?book_show_action=true">Feb 18, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="ELLIAS (elliasreads)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="ELLIAS (elliasreads)" href="/user/show/13699205-ellias-elliasreads">ELLIAS (elliasreads)</a>
      </span>
