<div id="review_2506066022" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2506066022" />
    <a title="Rochelle | Rochelle Reads ♡" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/20997898-rochelle-rochelle-reads"><img alt="Rochelle | Rochelle Reads ♡" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1580539086p2/20997898.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2506066022?book_show_action=true">Dec 31, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rochelle | Rochelle Reads ♡" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rochelle | Rochelle Reads ♡" href="/user/show/20997898-rochelle-rochelle-reads">Rochelle | Rochelle Reads ♡</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/20997898-rochelle-rochelle-reads?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2506066022" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11055920528386884425"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1546858354i/26878611.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>A story of a Nemesis and a Villain with no chance at a happy ending. Where the prince doesn't save the princess. He tortures her. And the beauty doesn't sleep. She's stuck. In a nightmare.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>What a fantastic beginning to reading in 2019! <br/><br/>I <i>knew</i> I’d fall in love with this, because it is L.J. Shen. One of, if not, my favourite author. Ever. She’s a proficient and excellent writer—her sentences are carefully and beautifully constructed into gripping scenes and concise prose—who continues t</span>
  <span id="freeText11055920528386884425" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1546858354i/26878611.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>A story of a Nemesis and a Villain with no chance at a happy ending. Where the prince doesn't save the princess. He tortures her. And the beauty doesn't sleep. She's stuck. In a nightmare.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>What a fantastic beginning to reading in 2019! <br><br>I <i>knew</i> I’d fall in love with this, because it is L.J. Shen. One of, if not, my favourite author. Ever. She’s a proficient and excellent writer—her sentences are carefully and beautifully constructed into gripping scenes and concise prose—who continues to astound me with every release. <br><br>She’s mastered an ability to transform cold-hearted and callous asshole heroes, who undergo an inevitable transformation of redemption, into loveable characters we can’t hate. They’re always damaged, filled with cynicism and sarcasm and hatred towards the wrongdoer, yet loaded with vengeance and countless positive qualities that make them <i>them</i>.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>God, she was sweet, and she was all mine. Not just her body but also her words and her courage.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I thought I loved Baron “Vicious” Spencer; adored Celian Laurent, but I’m unconditionally infatuated and unquestionably besotted with Wolfe Keaton—The Kiss Thief. On the surface, he appears to be nothing beyond ruthless; however, there’s an immense amount of depth, intrigue and enigma surrounding this mean anti-hero. Without doubt, he is complex and multi-faceted, someone who appears withdrawn and detached, yet beneath the tough exterior is someone able to love. And love hard. Fierce, without shame. Wild, without restraint.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>We were entwined and entangled, connected with invisible strings, each of us trying to pull away, only to create more knots that made us closer.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Francesca Rossi is my newest fictional best friend. Tangent: I was <i>almost</i> named Francesca. Ergo, we’re best friends. I digress. Having been raised dreadfully sheltered inside a gilded cage, oftentimes Francesca appears to be docile, unsure of herself and awfully immature. Seeming complaisant, or sometimes quiet, however, doesn’t always mean being submissive or feeble-minded—she’s quick-witted and intelligent. Torn between an older life bound in tradition and a newer life promising freedom, Francesca transforms into someone more daring, challenging and outspoken. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>He turned to me, his grays on my blues, two pools of beautiful lies.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Wolfe and Francesca are explosive. Passionate enemies who slowly and quietly transform into intimate lovers. Wrapped up in an unexpected fervid romance; embraced by an intense connection. <br><br><i>The Kiss Thief</i> is an engrossing, riveting narrative of an arranged marriage set within a modern Chicago. Promises of revenge shadowed by danger is abundant—you will be turning the pages faster than expected. L.J. Shen continues to astound me with the ways she illustrates love. It is always an intense fierceness of earnest affection and vicious yearning that is wretched and heart-aching however <i>real</i>. To be <i>in real love</i> is to be free. To change. To transform into someone greater than you’ve imagined. And she’s portrayed this through Wolfe and Francesca.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1524653840i/25430869.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Follow me on:</b> <a href="https://rochellereads.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/rochelle.reads/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="11055920528386884425" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17941610720463006520">I was lucky enough to read an ARC of the The Kiss Thief and let me tell you the chemistry between Keaton and Francesca is through the freaking roof. Once again, Ms Shen has created a damaged alpha, a-hole hero that I couldn't help but fall head over heels in love with.<br/><br/>Ms Shen has the amazing ability to take me through an entire emotional gamut. I wanted to throttle the hero and yet . . . I also wanted to ride him like a rodeo bull. My heart broke for Francesca and the impossible situation she fo</span>
  <span id="freeText17941610720463006520" style="display:none">I was lucky enough to read an ARC of the The Kiss Thief and let me tell you the chemistry between Keaton and Francesca is through the freaking roof. Once again, Ms Shen has created a damaged alpha, a-hole hero that I couldn't help but fall head over heels in love with.<br /><br />Ms Shen has the amazing ability to take me through an entire emotional gamut. I wanted to throttle the hero and yet . . . I also wanted to ride him like a rodeo bull. My heart broke for Francesca and the impossible situation she found herself in. I loved her strength and conviction as she came to terms with her reality, no matter how difficult and painful.<br /><br />This book is fabulous.<br /><br />I went on a brief historical reading binge after I finished it.<br /><br />And it's been months and I'm still thinking about it. And one scene in particular that will break your heart and show you, as the reader, just how strong the heroine is, and just how fully Ms Shen is able to draw you into the worlds she creates.<br /><br />The Kiss Thief is all the things I love about historical romance set in the contemporary world. It's emotional, sexy and heartbreaking and intense.<br /><br />I wish I could read it again for the first time</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7588637164619884398"><b>yeetus deletus </b><br/><br/>yeah i dunno, i usually sum up my thoughts in bold but i can't think of a good tag line for this book. first thoughts though: much better than dirty headlines (which is a book i wish i could forget forever).<br/><br/>i think i'm starting to realize a pattern with lj's books and tbh once i start seeing patterns it's all downhill from there. 98% of lj's heroes are dickheads. i mean BEYOND dickheads. and you always fall for them which is fine and dandy. except that it's really hard to believe </span>
  <span id="freeText7588637164619884398" style="display:none"><b>yeetus deletus </b><br /><br />yeah i dunno, i usually sum up my thoughts in bold but i can't think of a good tag line for this book. first thoughts though: much better than dirty headlines (which is a book i wish i could forget forever).<br /><br />i think i'm starting to realize a pattern with lj's books and tbh once i start seeing patterns it's all downhill from there. 98% of lj's heroes are dickheads. i mean BEYOND dickheads. and you always fall for them which is fine and dandy. except that it's really hard to believe in their love. she does this thing at like 80-90% into the book where the hero comes to this epiphany that he loves the heroine and it's always done the same way. like 2 pages of him waxing poetic on how he's treated her like garbage but he can't live without her.<br /><br />and that was barely ok the first time it showed up in her books, but it's getting hard to sympathize with after 3+ times. get creative, lady.<br /><br /><b>what didn't bug me</b><br /><br />you're going to see a lot of reviews mentioning other woman/other man drama. and there is. but it didn't really bother me. neither character truly cheats on the other. if anything it just shows how juvenile the two main characters are.<br /><br />beyond that, if the plot interests you at all i would say give this a try. it's certainly not a bad book it's just a little repetitive with the lack of trust and endless cycle of trying to one up each other. the chemistry is definitely there between the main characters tho.<br /><br />trigger warning though for: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[dubious consent when heroine is losing her virginity. it was mildly disturbing. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2665756535" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5855386686376169397">Ms. Shen has become one of my go to author for romance genre. Her books, for me, are something that I like to read in between my fantasy/historical fiction. They are fast paced, and a bit predictable but I like them. So when I found this on my new release by the authors that I have read, I was very excited. That cover and blurb, of course I was going to read it as soon as it was released. <br/><br/>Wolfe and Francesca's story is very much similar to <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/27263454.Sparrow' title='Sparrow by L.J. Shen' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sparrow</a>. A forced marriage where the couple slowly fell </span>
  <span id="freeText5855386686376169397" style="display:none">Ms. Shen has become one of my go to author for romance genre. Her books, for me, are something that I like to read in between my fantasy/historical fiction. They are fast paced, and a bit predictable but I like them. So when I found this on my new release by the authors that I have read, I was very excited. That cover and blurb, of course I was going to read it as soon as it was released. <br /><br />Wolfe and Francesca's story is very much similar to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/27263454.Sparrow" title="Sparrow by L.J. Shen" rel="nofollow noopener">Sparrow</a>. A forced marriage where the couple slowly fell in love. Like Shen's other heroes Wolfe is also a dominant male who likes to demean Francesca. He was a jerk to her for first half, all the while lusting after her. Things changed between them after a bad incident. And when I thought everything was going to be fine, Francesca had to go and do something so stupid to jeopardize their relation.<br /><br />Wolfe and Francesca both had their positive and negative points but I liked Wolfe a little more than Francesca because author gave Wolfe a great backstory. And the guy tried to be good to her but Francesca had a knack for pissing off Wolfe. She lived in her little fantasy world believing in things which ended up hurting both of them. <br /><br />So this book has it's ups and downs for me but I enjoyed reading it. Looking forward to next L J Shen now. </span>
  <a data-text-id="5855386686376169397" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer3745298021342728672"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br/><br/><b>Overall Opinion: </b>I enjoyed this. I just didn't enjoy it as much as I had hoped. I'm in the minority yet again here. I do really enjoy this author's ability to write a nasty H. And I enjoyed this H for the most part, but I think I just needed some more of the good to balance him out. I didn't like the fact that their dates were skimmed over. I think that would've helped a ton in redeeming him and his impulsively jerkish behavior! Yes, he groveled -- but because some of it felt skimmed ov</span>
  <span id="freeText3745298021342728672" style="display:none"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b>I enjoyed this. I just didn't enjoy it as much as I had hoped. I'm in the minority yet again here. I do really enjoy this author's ability to write a nasty H. And I enjoyed this H for the most part, but I think I just needed some more of the good to balance him out. I didn't like the fact that their dates were skimmed over. I think that would've helped a ton in redeeming him and his impulsively jerkish behavior! Yes, he groveled -- but because some of it felt skimmed over it didn't feel like enough for me. This also has some content that I'm sure some readers won't like, so please check out my spoiler tags below if you're considering reading but might have some "triggers" that would ruin a book for you. However, I think this will be a success -- especially with those readers that like this author's other works.<br /><br /><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Francesca and Wolfe's story. Francesca is the only daughter of a big crime boss. She meets Senator Wolfe Keaton on a night that she dreams is the night of her first kiss with the man she's been in love with for years. What she doesn't expect is that the jerk at her table would steal that kiss and then declare they are to be married the next day. Wolfe has a plot for revenge and Francesca's dad is the main target. They have a bumpy road, but the more time they spend together the more their walls start to fall and they fall in love...and get a HEA ending.<br /><br /><b>POV:</b> This alternated between Francesca and Wolfe's POV.<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b> Good. I never skimmed and I thought it flowed well.<br /><br /><b>Instalove:</b> No, they take a while to develop stronger feelings. More like hate-to-love.<br /><br /><b>H rating:</b> 3.5 stars. Wolfe. I liked him for the most part, but I had to deduct some for the impulsive jerkish behavior he displayed a few times.<br /><br /><b>h rating:</b> 3.5 stars. Francesca. I liked her, but I didn't like her indecisiveness towards the end and what she did to the H.<br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b>Low, no tissues needed<br /><br /><b>Push/Pull:</b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ They both push away at times (H more so), and I'd say that they both also pursue the relationship at times (also was the H more so).  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Good. They have some good tension, chemistry, and scenes -- but not so much it takes away from the story. Not as hot as I thought it'd be though.<br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> Yes<br /><br /><b>OW/OM drama:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ The h has a love interest when they meet. There is also a ex-fling of the H that causes some drama, and he goes out publicly with OW when they are married. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> No <br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The h publicly kisses old love while married to the H and after things had progressed between the h and H. The H slept with OW when they were first engaged because he thought the h slept with her love interest (and she also led him to believe that). The H also made the h believe that he was with OW after they are married and she publicly kisses OM, but he didn't go through with anything physical (just was publicly out) with OW. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Separation:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[They are separated shortly, but there was no mention or suggestion of other partners during this time.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Arranged marriage (on page), H is ~11 years older than the h, the h was a virgin and the H was a manwhore before the h, cheating (off and on page), criminal activity (off page), aggressive first sexual encounter that might feel borderline rape but he didn't know she was a virgin (on page), unexpected pregnancy (on page), and loss of loved ones (off page)  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Closure: </b> This had pretty good closure with what I would call a HEA ending <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[they're still married with children <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br /><br /><b>Safety:</b> This one is probably <u>Not Safe</u> for most safety gang readers depending on personal preferences.<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />- <b>Does </b> have cheating<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have a descriptive sex scene with OW/OM<br />- <b> Does</b> have both the h and H pushing away<br />- <b> Does</b> have a separation between the h and H<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have abuse<br />- <b>Does </b> have a HEA ending <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2513985075" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer11524851026954069989">Huge 5 stars for <i>The Kiss Thief</i>. This story was better than I expected and unique in many ways. Wolfe and Francesca are so hot together! Wolfe is alpha, dark, brooding and cold but the author shows us he is vulnerable and honorable. Francesca is sweet, innocent, smart and kind. Her beauty glows bright from within and out! She is really a lady but she is strong and a fighter as well! And she is caught in the middle of a fight between two men. If you really love someone, do you fight for them or l</span>
  <span id="freeText11524851026954069989" style="display:none">Huge 5 stars for <i>The Kiss Thief</i>. This story was better than I expected and unique in many ways. Wolfe and Francesca are so hot together! Wolfe is alpha, dark, brooding and cold but the author shows us he is vulnerable and honorable. Francesca is sweet, innocent, smart and kind. Her beauty glows bright from within and out! She is really a lady but she is strong and a fighter as well! And she is caught in the middle of a fight between two men. If you really love someone, do you fight for them or let them go? <br /><br />The author has done something fabulous. She created characters who I empathized with, whose actions alternately thrilled and horrified me, but most importantly they developed. The plot was excellent and had me engaged the whole time. It was well paced; nothing seemed too slow or too rushed. Really, there's a little bit of everything in here, and it mixes well to give you an exciting read. <br /><br />This book takes you into a whole new world with some great characters and a beautiful love story. High praise for L.J. Shen!<br /><br /><br /><u>In short:</u><br /><b>Hero</b> 5/5 | <b>Heroine</b> 5/5 | <b>Plot (Point, Originality)</b> 5/5 | <b>Writing Style</b> 5/5 | <b>Steam</b> 4/5 | <b>Romance</b> 5/5 | <b>Angst-Suspense</b> 4/5 | <b>Darkness</b> 2/5 | <b>Humor</b> 2/5 | <b>Secondary Characters</b> 5/5 | <b>Drama-Conflict</b> 5/5 | <b>Mystery</b> 0/5 | <b>Twists</b> 5/5 | <b>Pacing</b> Steady | <b>Action</b> 4/5<br />	<br /><br /><i>ARC kindly provided in exchange for an honest review.</i></span>

<div id="review_2506615686" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

        rated it

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/37433404-ninadonata-delfs?shelf=acrs">acrs</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2506615686" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4471844505071408425">First thing I was able to think about when this book hit my kindle, was to start the journey with these two characters. When I found out this book the book was coming I was so exited that sleeping was hard for me. The exitement for this book got to an unhealthy level.<br/>I’m so glad to say that this book was clearly worth my whole exitement.<br/>L.J. showed me a way of writing a love triangle in a way that didn't annoy me . Because most of the stories I’ve read until now which mostly had fantasy stories,</span>
  <span id="freeText4471844505071408425" style="display:none">First thing I was able to think about when this book hit my kindle, was to start the journey with these two characters. When I found out this book the book was coming I was so exited that sleeping was hard for me. The exitement for this book got to an unhealthy level.<br />I’m so glad to say that this book was clearly worth my whole exitement.<br />L.J. showed me a way of writing a love triangle in a way that didn't annoy me . Because most of the stories I’ve read until now which mostly had fantasy stories, the love triangles used to get on my nerves. So the author showed her talent with keeping up my interest in this love triangle.<br />I totally loved the way this story was constructed because in the beginning there had been a lot of hate. Then it changed. We saw how close love and hate can be together in relationships.<br />What made things more interesting was the position of our love interest.<br />All those feelings and those thoughts of the two main characters, L.J. Shen described in a way that I mostly was able to get why they acted like they did. Even if in some situations I wouldn’t act like they did.<br />Another fact that is amazing about the book that made me want to dive in the Story even if I really weren't in the mood for romance it was so hard to put this book down. Sometimes it seemed like I had a clue what will happen next but the the story went in an other way.<br />There were some passages in this book that brought me to tears and some that made me smirk. And even if these scenes had been really close together the author made it so I didn’t feel bad when I had to laugh.<br />There is a lot of character development placed in this story. <br /><br /><br />If you multiply Vics intention by ten you'll come out nearly to the total of how much of a bad boy Wolfe is. He can be very stubborn and grumpy. He knows what he can say at which time. Also he knows how deal with people who gave him pain. He likes it when every one is listening to his orders but also he has a soft side. Sometimes he shows humor and he loves fiercely, but hates with the same intensity.<br /><br />Francesca is a young woman who fights for her self and can be really sweet. She has like the author’s other heroines her way of being sassy. She always finds a way to make her self kind of happy. What is shown perfect by the words the author has choosen is how confused she is. There was so much strength in her.<br /><br />To conclude you can see that there was much about this boook I loved and the less time was left in that book the better the story got and the less in wanted to leave the characters. Even if I loved the relation to the American Italians in my eyes it was repeated to much. But it just costs this wonderful story just a quarter star. So we have 4.75 stars.<br />but I cant wait to read it again in a better condition.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4471844505071408425" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/61292418-anna-a-romance-reader?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2619652075" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16772599657805500327">If you know me you know how much I love L.J. Shen. She’s one of my favorite author’s of all time so when I read and saw the cover of The Kiss Thief I couldn’t contain my excitement. I am so sad to say that even though I enjoyed it, it fell kinda short for me. <br/><br/>Wolfe and Francesca’s sexual chemistry is off the charts from the moment they meet. I enjoyed their banter but I don’t know there was something missing. <br/><br/>SPOILERS AHEAD<br/><br/> <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[It bothers me that they always refer to her as a teenager</span></span>
  <span id="freeText16772599657805500327" style="display:none">If you know me you know how much I love L.J. Shen. She’s one of my favorite author’s of all time so when I read and saw the cover of The Kiss Thief I couldn’t contain my excitement. I am so sad to say that even though I enjoyed it, it fell kinda short for me. <br><br>Wolfe and Francesca’s sexual chemistry is off the charts from the moment they meet. I enjoyed their banter but I don’t know there was something missing. <br><br>SPOILERS AHEAD<br><br> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[It bothers me that they always refer to her as a teenager. She’s 19 and he’s 30. I understand there’s an age gap but please let it go. Its not like he’s an old guy. Even the H refers to her as a teenager and says things like “that’s what happens for marrying a teenager” Its a real turn off. I understand she’s young but she’s not a kid and they make it sound like she is. Also 30 is not old age. He’s still pretty young too. My parents married when my mom was 20 and my dad 30 and it wasn’t creepy. They are still happily married and about to celebrate their 41st anniversary. <br><br>Also whats up with Francesca always smoking? It would bother me too if he was the one smoking. The H even asked her not to smoke in the house but she still does. Also she was in a car accident and the first thing she asks the H is for a cigarette. Maybe its just me but smoking is a turn off, specially when they do it constantly. <br><br>I didn’t like that Wolfe had sex with OW after meeting Francesca. Also Francesca shouldn’t have kissed Angelo when she was already married. There’s just too much OW/OM drama for my liking. <br><br>These were just some of the things that didn’t sit well with me. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br>Overall the writing is amazing as usual but I was expecting more from this book. I did enjoy it but didn't love it. I will always love L.J. Shen and read everything she writes cause she's an amazing author. Can’t wait for her future books.<br><br><a href="http://aromancereader.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1503974782i/23711934._SX540_.png" alt="arc" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_2581428488" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2581428488" />
    <a title="Sophia Triad" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad"><img alt="Sophia Triad" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591419108p2/44642860.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2581428488?book_show_action=true">Nov 02, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sophia Triad" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sophia Triad" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad">Sophia Triad</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=2contemporary-lovestories">2contemporary-lovestories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=crime-mafia">crime-mafia</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2581428488" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2126542475953959417">It's been a while since I read this book, but I still remember everything about the story. So, I am sure this means that it was a great and very entertaining experience. <br/><br/>Maybe the reason that I loved it so much is that I also love Harlequin Presents books. <br/>There are so many similarities between this kind of books and The Kiss Thief.<br/><br/>Let's see:<br/>1.	Arranged marriage with an unwilling bride who loves someone else.<br/>2.	There is the virgin trope that it is valued more than anything. If the girl is no vir</span>
  <span id="freeText2126542475953959417" style="display:none">It's been a while since I read this book, but I still remember everything about the story. So, I am sure this means that it was a great and very entertaining experience. <br /><br />Maybe the reason that I loved it so much is that I also love Harlequin Presents books. <br />There are so many similarities between this kind of books and The Kiss Thief.<br /><br />Let's see:<br />1.	Arranged marriage with an unwilling bride who loves someone else.<br />2.	There is the virgin trope that it is valued more than anything. If the girl is no virgin and she had a few boyfriends at the boarding school, then obviously she is a slut LOL<br />3.	She never tells her husband of course, because... I am not sure why she never tells him. Many reasons we find in Harlequin romance books. She hates him. He hates her. She doesn't want to confide in him. She is embarrassed. She is sure that when he finds out he will be embarrassed. And this is payback somehow. Hmmm... etc etc etc<br />4.	Then, when the jealous husband realises that she is a virgin the first time they have sex, he is surprised, he is astonished, he is proud that he was the first who conquered her. You know the drill. Fun stuff.<br />5.	There are so many MISUNDERSTANDINGS! She loves someone else. He sleeps around. He only wants her to avenge her father and he never loved her. She wants to escape and she never loved him.<br />6.	There is this revenge issue obviously. He is not a bad man. The circumstances made him a bad man who likes to torture her.<br />7.	And suddenly the man-whore becomes the most faithful husband. He cannot get it up for another woman, even when he tries.<br />8.	A jealous ex girlfriend always appears messing things up.<br />9.	Don't forget the unexpected pregnancy. Needless to say they don't know what happened. They were so careful. They counted the fertility days. Who needs a condom or a pill?<br />10.	Grovelling. Enough grovelling to satisfy you.<br />11.	And there is a glorious happily ever after. All the bad people are away and miserable. All the nice people are around and happy.<br /><br />Well, I think that is the whole story. <br />Thus if you expect a dark and broody romance, I think you will be dissatisfied. <br />Also if you expect a love triangle, you will also be disappointed. The ex boyfriend and almost ex fiancé is totally unimportant. No angst there people.<br /><br />But if you are thirsty for the things that I mentioned above. If you are thrilled with passionate love stories that no necessarily end up with drama, then you will love this book as much as I did.<br /><br />By far my favourite quote from the book:<br /><b>
  <i>“You know I respect you,” he said gruffly.<br />“I know,” I murmured, my lips swollen and sensitive.<br />“Good. Because for the next five seconds, it’s going to look like I don’t.”</i>
</b><br />😏<br /><br /><br />.....................................<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />BEFORE PUBLICATION <br /><br />COVER &amp; BLURB REVEAL! (6th Decemb)<br /><br /><i>They say your first kiss should be earned.<br /><br />Mine was stolen by a devil in a masquerade mask under the black Chicago sky.<br /><br />They say the vows you take on your wedding day are sacred.<br /><br />Mine were broken before we left church.<br /><br />They say your heart only beats for one man.<br /><br />Mine split and bled for two rivals who fought for it until the bitter end.<br /><br />I was promised to Angelo Bandini, the heir to one of the most powerful families in the Chicago Outfit.<br /><br />Then taken by Senator Wolfe Keaton, who held my father’s sins over his head to force me into marriage.  <br /><br />They say that all great love stories have a happy ending.<br /><br />I, Francesca Rossi, found myself erasing and rewriting mine until the very last chapter.<br /><br />One kiss.<br />Two men.<br />Three lives.<br />Entwined together.<br /><br />And somewhere between these two men, I had to find my forever. </i><br /><br /><br />-----------------------------<br /><i>I felll in love with two men.<br />Two, imperfect men.<br />Two men<br />Who happened to hate each other. </i><br /><br />Super excited for this book! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>
  <a data-text-id="2126542475953959417" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('aZqCVUnMvyL24Q/0rxhPcpMCN50tU8uB4Ceq9+gCDmieEvRYQHPEgc/x4g6GBxdMkwT3tEkZ0pT6J+sX5RRVJw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('zwWs3559VENS7QtYO+ZQJ5Qmo7WSP8du+Xy8sCcN9DI4jdrSl8Iv4Gv95qIS+QgZlCBjnPZ13nvjfP1QKhuvfQ==')})
  }
